He advised getting a new one rather than trying to trick me into paying him hundreds of dollars to do a fix that might not work.

Fantastic place!

I ended up with the chicken lettuce cups, minus the noodles.  Service was prompt and friendly, but the food was only okay. I have to say I have been to many Vietnamese restaurants and stayed in Vietnam for 1 month before. This place always makes me happy. The atmosphere is nothing fancy but clean. Service is always good most understand English. Personally I love their egg rolls (Cha Gio) and their shaken beef (bo luc lac). I also enjoy the rice vermicelli bowls (bun) the beef is my fav. If your looking for a fresh drink I'd recommend trying a soda lemonade (soda Chanh) basically fresh lime with sugar and soda. Parking is also easy in the large lot the plaza its in has. If your looking for a great all around Vietnamese restaurant this is a good choice. I think they make all dishes very well.<//text>

When I dropped off my 2019 Chevy Tahoe LT, I told the service writer the problem I was having. The problem was my auto insurance company text me stating that I had (3) error codes on my Tahoe. The service writer asks me if the service warning light was on, and I told him it wasn't on. He said if the light wasn't on that there are no code errors probably are none existing.

After testing for error codes, the service writer was correct. There were no existing error codes. The past error code data was not cleared which the insurance company was receiving on there end.

So, my experience with Merced Chevrolet was great. The service writer was very friendly, knowledgeable, and experienced.

Thank Merced Chevrolet, job well done.</text>

We purchased a car from this dealership yesterday, and it was without a doubt the WORST CAR BUYING EXPERIENCE EVER.  I want to say that I have bought a few cars but never left so disappointed as I did yesterday.  Rick was the sales associate, and my husband and I had already done some searching before we reached the lot and had two cars specifically in mind, we let Rick know this and he took us to the two cars we had inquired about.  After test driving and briefly discussing the two cars we decided that we wanted to purchase a car from this dealer.  Rick took us into the lobby to have a seat and talk financing.  We started off by letting Rick know that we were already pre-approved by our own bank with a bankruptcy on our history at a rate of 3.99% so we asked him to start by running our information and seeing if they could beat the rate with a different bank since we knew they were part of the CUDL system.  Rick proceeded to inform us that "We like to see some kind of down payment with this kind of purchase, so what were you thinking? They like to see something like $4,000." We let him know that was not a problem if that was the route we took but again said that we would like him to just start by trying to beat the rate we had been pre-approved for.  He then goes into the office of a gentleman in charge of getting us pre-approved and after a few seconds comes back out with a print out with the break down of what we would be paying, how much our payment would be and so on.  I noticed at the top it had the same rate of 3.99% so I asked Rick, "Does that mean you guys couldn't beat the rate?" and he replies nonchalantly "We didn't even try..." so we review the print out and we ask him to make some adjustments, he takes the paperwork back and comes out with a new print out and we review it one more time at this point Rick asks, "Do we have a deal?" and I say "fill up the tank, wash the car and you have a deal."  Anyone who has bought a car before would think this is a reasonable offer BUT NO he comes back with, "We don't do that for used cars, only new ones because we can get reimbursed, and the car wash will be about thirty minutes."  We proceed with purchasing the car because we knew regardless of the service we were receiving this was still a good deal for the car we bought.  Mayra B. was great she was friendly, prompt and efficient.  She was the only good part of the whole experience. After we finished we were walked out to the car by Rick who at this point was extremely friendly (unlike before) and once we got to the car he did offer to go over some things about the car but we declined, and he once again asked us to take the time to at least activate our 3 month free trial of OnStar because if we don't he would hear it from GM, but we had already told him we were not interested.  Today I called Ray Tarelli who is the Sales Manager hoping that Ray would try to make it right but he did not express an ounce of empathy towards our experience yesterday.  He actually went so far as to say that it was our fault because we didn't let Rick do his job, when I asked what he meant he said, "Rick was trying to set up your OnStar and you wouldn't let him because you were in such a hurry."HE EVEN HUNG UP ON ME!!! We had already expressed that we were not interested in signing up for something we were never intending to use/purchase.  I then called back and asked if there was someone else that I could speak to a few minutes later I got a call from the owner Will.  Will was nice, I felt at some points he was trying to defend his employees and their actions BUT he tried to make it right by offering to set up an appointment to wash the car and fill our tank but I had to decline, after everything was said and done it came down to the principle, the way Will handled my complaint should have been the way Ray and Rick tried to handle it.  This is not how you treat customers and I will never recommend this dealership to anyone.  Seek a car elsewhere!!!< /review>
